140/* checks if <err> is a real error for errno or one that can be ignored, and
141 * return 0 for these ones or <err> for real ones.
142 */
143static inline int unclean_errno(int err)
144{
145 if (err == EAGAIN11 || err == EINPROGRESS115 ||
146 err == EISCONN106 || err == EALREADY114)
147 return 0;
148 return err;
149}

151/*
152 * Convert check_status code to description
153 */
154const char *get_check_status_description(short check_status) {
155
156 const char *desc;
157
158 if (check_status < HCHK_STATUS_SIZE)
159 desc = check_statuses[check_status].desc;
160 else
161 desc = NULL((void*)0);
162
163 if (desc && *desc)
164 return desc;
165 else
166 return check_statuses[HCHK_STATUS_UNKNOWN].desc;
167}

170 * Convert check_status code to short info

172const char *get_check_status_info(short check_status) {
173
174 const char *info;
175
176 if (check_status < HCHK_STATUS_SIZE)
177 info = check_statuses[check_status].info;
178 else
179 info = NULL((void*)0);
180
181 if (info && *info)
182 return info;
183 else
184 return check_statuses[HCHK_STATUS_UNKNOWN].info;
185}

202/*
203 * Set check->status, update check->duration and fill check->result with
204 * an adequate CHK_RES_* value. The new check->health is computed based
205 * on the result.
206 *
207 * Show information in logs about failed health check if server is UP
208 * or succeeded health checks if server is DOWN.
209 */
210static void set_server_check_status(struct check *check, short status, const char *desc)
211{
212 struct server *s = check->server;
213 short prev_status = check->status;
214 int report = 0;
215
216 if (status == HCHK_STATUS_START) {
217 check->result = CHK_RES_UNKNOWN; /* no result yet */
218 check->desc[0] = '\0';
219 check->start = now;
220 return;
221 }
222
223 if (!check->status)
224 return;
225
226 if (desc && *desc) {
227 strncpy(check->desc, desc, HCHK_DESC_LEN128-1);
228 check->desc[HCHK_DESC_LEN128-1] = '\0';
229 } else
230 check->desc[0] = '\0';
231
232 check->status = status;
233 if (check_statuses[status].result)
234 check->result = check_statuses[status].result;
235
236 if (status == HCHK_STATUS_HANA)
237 check->duration = -1;
238 else if (!tv_iszero(&check->start)(((&check->start)->tv_sec | (&check->start)->
tv_usec) == 0)) {
239 /* set_server_check_status() may be called more than once */
240 check->duration = tv_ms_elapsed__tv_ms_elapsed(&check->start, &now);
241 tv_zero(&check->start);
242 }
243
244 /* no change is expected if no state change occurred */
245 if (check->result == CHK_RES_NEUTRAL)
246 return;
247
248 /* If the check was really just sending a mail, it won't have an
249 * associated server, so we're done now.
250 */
251 if (!s)
252 return;
253 report = 0;
254
255 switch (check->result) {
256 case CHK_RES_FAILED:
257 /* Failure to connect to the agent as a secondary check should not
258 * cause the server to be marked down.
259 */
260 if ((!(check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010) ||
261 (check->status >= HCHK_STATUS_L57DATA)) &&
262 (check->health > 0)) {
263 _HA_ATOMIC_ADD(&s->counters.failed_checks, 1)__atomic_add_fetch(&s->counters.failed_checks, 1, 0);
264 report = 1;
265 check->health--;
266 if (check->health < check->rise)
267 check->health = 0;
268 }
269 break;
270
271 case CHK_RES_PASSED:
272 case CHK_RES_CONDPASS: /* "condpass" cannot make the first step but it OK after a "passed" */
273 if ((check->health < check->rise + check->fall - 1) &&
274 (check->result == CHK_RES_PASSED || check->health > 0)) {
275 report = 1;
276 check->health++;
277
278 if (check->health >= check->rise)
279 check->health = check->rise + check->fall - 1; /* OK now */
280 }
281
282 /* clear consecutive_errors if observing is enabled */
283 if (s->onerror)
284 s->consecutive_errors = 0;
285 break;
286
287 default:
288 break;
289 }
290
291 if (s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_LOGHCHKS0x00000800 &&
292 (status != prev_status || report)) {
293 chunk_printf(&trash,
294 "%s check for %sserver %s/%s %s%s",
295 (check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010) ? "Agent" : "Health",
296 s->flags & SRV_F_BACKUP0x0001 ? "backup " : "",
297 s->proxy->id, s->id,
298 (check->result == CHK_RES_CONDPASS) ? "conditionally ":"",
299 (check->result >= CHK_RES_PASSED) ? "succeeded" : "failed");
300
301 srv_append_status(&trash, s, check, -1, 0);
302
303 chunk_appendf(&trash, ", status: %d/%d %s",
304 (check->health >= check->rise) ? check->health - check->rise + 1 : check->health,
305 (check->health >= check->rise) ? check->fall : check->rise,
306 (check->health >= check->rise) ? (s->uweight ? "UP" : "DRAIN") : "DOWN");
307
308 ha_warning("%s.\n", trash.area);
309 send_log(s->proxy, LOG_NOTICE5, "%s.\n", trash.area);
310 send_email_alert(s, LOG_INFO6, "%s", trash.area);
311 }
312}
313
314/* Marks the check <check>'s server down if the current check is already failed
315 * and the server is not down yet nor in maintenance.
316 */
317static void check_notify_failure(struct check *check)
318{
319 struct server *s = check->server;
320
321 /* The agent secondary check should only cause a server to be marked
322 * as down if check->status is HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, which indicates
323 * that the agent returned "fail", "stopped" or "down".
324 * The implication here is that failure to connect to the agent
325 * as a secondary check should not cause the server to be marked
326 * down. */
327 if ((check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010) && check->status != HCHK_STATUS_L7STS)
328 return;
329
330 if (check->health > 0)
331 return;
332
333 /* We only report a reason for the check if we did not do so previously */
334 srv_set_stopped(s, NULL((void*)0), (!s->track && !(s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_LOGHCHKS0x00000800)) ? check : NULL((void*)0));
335}
336
337/* Marks the check <check> as valid and tries to set its server up, provided
338 * it isn't in maintenance, it is not tracking a down server and other checks
339 * comply. The rule is simple : by default, a server is up, unless any of the
340 * following conditions is true :
341 * - health check failed (check->health < rise)
342 * - agent check failed (agent->health < rise)
343 * - the server tracks a down server (track && track->state == STOPPED)
344 * Note that if the server has a slowstart, it will switch to STARTING instead
345 * of RUNNING. Also, only the health checks support the nolb mode, so the
346 * agent's success may not take the server out of this mode.
347 */
348static void check_notify_success(struct check *check)
349{
350 struct server *s = check->server;
351
352 if (s->next_admin & SRV_ADMF_MAINT)
353 return;
354
355 if (s->track && s->track->next_state == SRV_ST_STOPPED)
356 return;
357
358 if ((s->check.state & CHK_ST_ENABLED0x0004) && (s->check.health < s->check.rise))
359 return;
360
361 if ((s->agent.state & CHK_ST_ENABLED0x0004) && (s->agent.health < s->agent.rise))
362 return;
363
364 if ((check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010) && s->next_state == SRV_ST_STOPPING)
365 return;
366
367 srv_set_running(s, NULL((void*)0), (!s->track && !(s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_LOGHCHKS0x00000800)) ? check : NULL((void*)0));
368}
369
370/* Marks the check <check> as valid and tries to set its server into stopping mode
371 * if it was running or starting, and provided it isn't in maintenance and other
372 * checks comply. The conditions for the server to be marked in stopping mode are
373 * the same as for it to be turned up. Also, only the health checks support the
374 * nolb mode.
375 */
376static void check_notify_stopping(struct check *check)
377{
378 struct server *s = check->server;
379
380 if (s->next_admin & SRV_ADMF_MAINT)
381 return;
382
383 if (check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010)
384 return;
385
386 if (s->track && s->track->next_state == SRV_ST_STOPPED)
387 return;
388
389 if ((s->check.state & CHK_ST_ENABLED0x0004) && (s->check.health < s->check.rise))
390 return;
391
392 if ((s->agent.state & CHK_ST_ENABLED0x0004) && (s->agent.health < s->agent.rise))
393 return;
394
395 srv_set_stopping(s, NULL((void*)0), (!s->track && !(s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_LOGHCHKS0x00000800)) ? check : NULL((void*)0));
396}
397
398/* note: use health_adjust() only, which first checks that the observe mode is
399 * enabled.
400 */
401void __health_adjust(struct server *s, short status)
402{
403 int failed;
404 int expire;
405
406 if (s->observe >= HANA_OBS_SIZE)
407 return;
408
409 if (status >= HANA_STATUS_SIZE || !analyze_statuses[status].desc)
410 return;
411
412 switch (analyze_statuses[status].lr[s->observe - 1]) {
413 case 1:
414 failed = 1;
415 break;
416
417 case 2:
418 failed = 0;
419 break;
420
421 default:
422 return;
423 }
424
425 if (!failed) {
426 /* good: clear consecutive_errors */
427 s->consecutive_errors = 0;
428 return;
429 }
430
431 _HA_ATOMIC_ADD(&s->consecutive_errors, 1)__atomic_add_fetch(&s->consecutive_errors, 1, 0);
432
433 if (s->consecutive_errors < s->consecutive_errors_limit)
434 return;
435
436 chunk_printf(&trash, "Detected %d consecutive errors, last one was: %s",
437 s->consecutive_errors, get_analyze_status(status));
438
439 switch (s->onerror) {
440 case HANA_ONERR_FASTINTER:
441 /* force fastinter - nothing to do here as all modes force it */
442 break;
443
444 case HANA_ONERR_SUDDTH:
445 /* simulate a pre-fatal failed health check */
446 if (s->check.health > s->check.rise)
447 s->check.health = s->check.rise + 1;
448
449 /* no break - fall through */
450
451 case HANA_ONERR_FAILCHK:
452 /* simulate a failed health check */
453 set_server_check_status(&s->check, HCHK_STATUS_HANA,
454 trash.area);
455 check_notify_failure(&s->check);
456 break;
457
458 case HANA_ONERR_MARKDWN:
459 /* mark server down */
460 s->check.health = s->check.rise;
461 set_server_check_status(&s->check, HCHK_STATUS_HANA,
462 trash.area);
463 check_notify_failure(&s->check);
464 break;
465
466 default:
467 /* write a warning? */
468 break;
469 }
470
471 s->consecutive_errors = 0;
472 _HA_ATOMIC_ADD(&s->counters.failed_hana, 1)__atomic_add_fetch(&s->counters.failed_hana, 1, 0);
473
474 if (s->check.fastinter) {
475 expire = tick_add(now_ms, MS_TO_TICKS(s->check.fastinter)(s->check.fastinter));
476 if (s->check.task->expire > expire) {
477 s->check.task->expire = expire;
478 /* requeue check task with new expire */
479 task_queue(s->check.task);
480 }
481 }
482}

484static int httpchk_build_status_header(struct server *s, char *buffer, int size)
485{
486 int sv_state;
487 int ratio;
488 int hlen = 0;
489 char addr[46];
490 char port[6];
491 const char *srv_hlt_st[7] = { "DOWN", "DOWN %d/%d",
492 "UP %d/%d", "UP",
493 "NOLB %d/%d", "NOLB",
494 "no check" };
495
496 memcpy(buffer + hlen, "X-Haproxy-Server-State: ", 24);
497 hlen += 24;
498
499 if (!(s->check.state & CHK_ST_ENABLED0x0004))
500 sv_state = 6;
501 else if (s->cur_state != SRV_ST_STOPPED) {
502 if (s->check.health == s->check.rise + s->check.fall - 1)
503 sv_state = 3; /* UP */
504 else
505 sv_state = 2; /* going down */
506
507 if (s->cur_state == SRV_ST_STOPPING)
508 sv_state += 2;
509 } else {
510 if (s->check.health)
511 sv_state = 1; /* going up */
512 else
513 sv_state = 0; /* DOWN */
514 }
515
516 hlen += snprintf(buffer + hlen, size - hlen,
517 srv_hlt_st[sv_state],
518 (s->cur_state != SRV_ST_STOPPED) ? (s->check.health - s->check.rise + 1) : (s->check.health),
519 (s->cur_state != SRV_ST_STOPPED) ? (s->check.fall) : (s->check.rise));
520
521 addr_to_str(&s->addr, addr, sizeof(addr));
522 if (s->addr.ss_family == AF_INET2 || s->addr.ss_family == AF_INET610)
523 snprintf(port, sizeof(port), "%u", s->svc_port);
524 else
525 *port = 0;
526
527 hlen += snprintf(buffer + hlen, size - hlen, "; address=%s; port=%s; name=%s/%s; node=%s; weight=%d/%d; scur=%d/%d; qcur=%d",
528 addr, port, s->proxy->id, s->id,
529 global.node,
530 (s->cur_eweight * s->proxy->lbprm.wmult + s->proxy->lbprm.wdiv - 1) / s->proxy->lbprm.wdiv,
531 (s->proxy->lbprm.tot_weight * s->proxy->lbprm.wmult + s->proxy->lbprm.wdiv - 1) / s->proxy->lbprm.wdiv,
532 s->cur_sess, s->proxy->beconn - s->proxy->nbpend,
533 s->nbpend);
534
535 if ((s->cur_state == SRV_ST_STARTING) &&
536 now.tv_sec < s->last_change + s->slowstart &&
537 now.tv_sec >= s->last_change) {
538 ratio = MAX(1, 100 * (now.tv_sec - s->last_change) / s->slowstart)(((1)>(100 * (now.tv_sec - s->last_change) / s->slowstart
))?(1):(100 * (now.tv_sec - s->last_change) / s->slowstart
));
539 hlen += snprintf(buffer + hlen, size - hlen, "; throttle=%d%%", ratio);
540 }
541
542 buffer[hlen++] = '\r';
543 buffer[hlen++] = '\n';
544
545 return hlen;
546}
547
548/* Check the connection. If an error has already been reported or the socket is
549 * closed, keep errno intact as it is supposed to contain the valid error code.
550 * If no error is reported, check the socket's error queue using getsockopt().
551 * Warning, this must be done only once when returning from poll, and never
552 * after an I/O error was attempted, otherwise the error queue might contain
553 * inconsistent errors. If an error is detected, the CO_FL_ERROR is set on the
554 * socket. Returns non-zero if an error was reported, zero if everything is
555 * clean (including a properly closed socket).
556 */
557static int retrieve_errno_from_socket(struct connection *conn)
558{
559 int skerr;
560 socklen_t lskerr = sizeof(skerr);
561
562 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR && (unclean_errno(errno(*__errno_location ())) || !conn->ctrl))
563 return 1;
564
565 if (!conn_ctrl_ready(conn))
566 return 0;
567
568 if (getsockopt(conn->handle.fd, SOL_SOCKET1, SO_ERROR4, &skerr, &lskerr) == 0)
569 errno(*__errno_location ()) = skerr;
570
571 errno(*__errno_location ()) = unclean_errno(errno(*__errno_location ()));
572
573 if (!errno(*__errno_location ())) {
574 /* we could not retrieve an error, that does not mean there is
575 * none. Just don't change anything and only report the prior
576 * error if any.
577 */
578 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR)
579 return 1;
580 else
581 return 0;
582 }
583
584 conn->flags |= CO_FL_ERROR | CO_FL_SOCK_WR_SH | CO_FL_SOCK_RD_SH;
585 return 1;
586}
587
588/* Try to collect as much information as possible on the connection status,
589 * and adjust the server status accordingly. It may make use of <errno_bck>
590 * if non-null when the caller is absolutely certain of its validity (eg:
591 * checked just after a syscall). If the caller doesn't have a valid errno,
592 * it can pass zero, and retrieve_errno_from_socket() will be called to try
593 * to extract errno from the socket. If no error is reported, it will consider
594 * the <expired> flag. This is intended to be used when a connection error was
595 * reported in conn->flags or when a timeout was reported in <expired>. The
596 * function takes care of not updating a server status which was already set.
597 * All situations where at least one of <expired> or CO_FL_ERROR are set
598 * produce a status.
599 */
600static void chk_report_conn_err(struct check *check, int errno_bck, int expired)
601{
602 struct conn_stream *cs = check->cs;
603 struct connection *conn = cs_conn(cs);
604 const char *err_msg;
605 struct buffer *chk;
606 int step;
607 char *comment;
608
609 if (check->result != CHK_RES_UNKNOWN)
610 return;
611
612 errno(*__errno_location ()) = unclean_errno(errno_bck);
613 if (conn && errno(*__errno_location ()))
614 retrieve_errno_from_socket(conn);
615
616 if (conn && !(conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR) &&
617 !(cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR) && !expired)
618 return;
619
620 /* we'll try to build a meaningful error message depending on the
621 * context of the error possibly present in conn->err_code, and the
622 * socket error possibly collected above. This is useful to know the
623 * exact step of the L6 layer (eg: SSL handshake).
624 */
625 chk = get_trash_chunk();
626
627 if (check->type == PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000) {
628 step = tcpcheck_get_step_id(check);
629 if (!step)
630 chunk_printf(chk, " at initial connection step of tcp-check");
631 else {
632 chunk_printf(chk, " at step %d of tcp-check", step);
633 /* we were looking for a string */
634 if (check->last_started_step && check->last_started_step->action == TCPCHK_ACT_CONNECT) {
635 if (check->last_started_step->port)
636 chunk_appendf(chk, " (connect port %d)" ,check->last_started_step->port);
637 else
638 chunk_appendf(chk, " (connect)");
639 }
640 else if (check->last_started_step && check->last_started_step->action == TCPCHK_ACT_EXPECT) {
641 if (check->last_started_step->string)
642 chunk_appendf(chk, " (expect string '%s')", check->last_started_step->string);
643 else if (check->last_started_step->expect_regex)
644 chunk_appendf(chk, " (expect regex)");
645 }
646 else if (check->last_started_step && check->last_started_step->action == TCPCHK_ACT_SEND) {
647 chunk_appendf(chk, " (send)");
648 }
649
650 comment = tcpcheck_get_step_comment(check, step);
651 if (comment)
652 chunk_appendf(chk, " comment: '%s'", comment);
653 }
654 }
655
656 if (conn && conn->err_code) {
657 if (unclean_errno(errno(*__errno_location ())))
658 chunk_printf(&trash, "%s (%s)%s", conn_err_code_str(conn), strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())),
659 chk->area);
660 else
661 chunk_printf(&trash, "%s%s", conn_err_code_str(conn),
662 chk->area);
663 err_msg = trash.area;
664 }
665 else {
666 if (unclean_errno(errno(*__errno_location ()))) {
667 chunk_printf(&trash, "%s%s", strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())),
668 chk->area);
669 err_msg = trash.area;
670 }
671 else {
672 err_msg = chk->area;
673 }
674 }
675
676 if (check->state & CHK_ST_PORT_MISS0x0020) {
677 /* NOTE: this is reported after <fall> tries */
678 chunk_printf(chk, "No port available for the TCP connection");
679 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_SOCKERR, err_msg);
680 }
681
682 if (!conn) {
683 /* connection allocation error before the connection was established */
684 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_SOCKERR, err_msg);
685 }
686 else if (conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_L4_CONN) {
687 /* L4 not established (yet) */
688 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR)
689 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L4CON, err_msg);
690 else if (expired)
691 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L4TOUT, err_msg);
692
693 /*
694 * might be due to a server IP change.
695 * Let's trigger a DNS resolution if none are currently running.
696 */
697 if (check->server)
698 dns_trigger_resolution(check->server->dns_requester);
699
700 }
701 else if (conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_L6_CONN) {
702 /* L6 not established (yet) */
703 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR)
704 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6RSP, err_msg);
705 else if (expired)
706 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6TOUT, err_msg);
707 }
708 else if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR) {
709 /* I/O error after connection was established and before we could diagnose */
710 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_SOCKERR, err_msg);
711 }
712 else if (expired) {
713 /* connection established but expired check */
714 if (check->type == PR_O2_SSL3_CHK0x70000000)
715 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6TOUT, err_msg);
716 else /* HTTP, SMTP, ... */
717 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7TOUT, err_msg);
718 }
719
720 return;
721}
722

short)(0x0000000100000000ULL + 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"
); } else if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) == 1)
{ asm volatile("lock subb %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&check->

+ 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"); } else { void __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_sub__
(char *,int); if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) !=
1 && sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) != 2 &&
sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) != 4 && (sizeof
(long) != 8 || sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) != 8
)) __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_sub__("src/checks.c",740
); } }); }) : (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) == 4
) ? ({ ({ if (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof(*(&check
->server->lock)) == 8) { asm volatile("lock subq %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned
long)(0x00010000 + 0x00000004)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*
(&check->server->lock)) == 4) { asm volatile("lock subl %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned

: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned

4 && (sizeof(long) != 8 || sizeof(*(&check->server
->lock)) != 8)) __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_drop_s__
("src/checks.c",740); }) );
741 else
742 HA_SPIN_UNLOCK(EMAIL_ALERTS_LOCK, &q->lock)( (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof(*(&q->lock)) ==
8) ? ({ ({ if (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof(*(&q->

)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*(&q->lock)) == 1) { asm

,742); } }); }) : (sizeof(*(&q->lock)) == 4) ? ({ ({ if

) { asm volatile("lock subq %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&q->lock
)) : "er" ((unsigned long)(0x00010000 + 0x00000004)) : "cc");

: "+m" (*(&q->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned int)(0x00010000
+ 0x00000004)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*(&q->lock)
) == 2) { asm volatile("lock subw %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&q->
lock)) : "er" ((unsigned short)(0x00010000 + 0x00000004)) : "cc"
); } else if (sizeof(*(&q->lock)) == 1) { asm volatile
("lock subb %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&q->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned
char)(0x00010000 + 0x00000004)) : "cc"); } else { void __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_sub__
(char *,int); if (sizeof(*(&q->lock)) != 1 && sizeof
(*(&q->lock)) != 2 && sizeof(*(&q->lock
)) != 4 && (sizeof(long) != 8 || sizeof(*(&q->
lock)) != 8)) __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_sub__("src/checks.c"
,742); } }); }) : ({ void __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_drop_s__
(char *,int); if (sizeof(*(&q->lock)) != 4 && (
sizeof(long) != 8 || sizeof(*(&q->lock)) != 8)) __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_drop_s__
("src/checks.c",742); }) );
743 }
744 return NULL((void*)0);
745}
746
747/* same as above but protected by the server lock.
748 *
749 * Please do NOT place any return statement in this function and only leave
750 * via the out label. NOTE THAT THIS FUNCTION DOESN'T LOCK, YOU PROBABLY WANT
751 * TO USE event_srv_chk_w() instead.
752 */
753static void __event_srv_chk_w(struct conn_stream *cs)
754{
755 struct connection *conn = cs->conn;
756 struct check *check = cs->data;
757 struct server *s = check->server;
758 struct task *t = check->task;
759
760 if (unlikely(check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED)(__builtin_expect((check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED) != 0, 0
)))
761 goto out_wakeup;
762
763 if (retrieve_errno_from_socket(conn)) {
764 chk_report_conn_err(check, errno(*__errno_location ()), 0);
765 goto out_wakeup;
766 }
767
768 /* here, we know that the connection is established. That's enough for
769 * a pure TCP check.
770 */
771 if (!check->type)
772 goto out_wakeup;
773
774 /* wake() will take care of calling tcpcheck_main() */
775 if (check->type == PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000)
776 goto out;
777
778 if (b_data(&check->bo)) {
779 cs->conn->mux->snd_buf(cs, &check->bo, b_data(&check->bo), 0);
780 b_realign_if_empty(&check->bo);
781 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR) {
782 chk_report_conn_err(check, errno(*__errno_location ()), 0);
783 goto out_wakeup;
784 }
785 if (b_data(&check->bo)) {
786 conn->mux->subscribe(cs, SUB_RETRY_SEND, &check->wait_list);
787 goto out;
788 }
789 }
790
791 /* full request sent, we allow up to <timeout.check> if nonzero for a response */
792 if (s->proxy->timeout.check) {
793 t->expire = tick_add_ifset(now_ms, s->proxy->timeout.check);
794 task_queue(t);
795 }
796 goto out;
797
798 out_wakeup:
799 task_wakeup(t, TASK_WOKEN_IO0x0400);
800 out:
801 return;
802}
803
804/*
805 * This function is used only for server health-checks. It handles the server's
806 * reply to an HTTP request, SSL HELLO or MySQL client Auth. It calls
807 * set_server_check_status() to update check->status, check->duration
808 * and check->result.
809
810 * The set_server_check_status function is called with HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD if
811 * an HTTP server replies HTTP 2xx or 3xx (valid responses), if an SMTP server
812 * returns 2xx, HCHK_STATUS_L6OK if an SSL server returns at least 5 bytes in
813 * response to an SSL HELLO (the principle is that this is enough to
814 * distinguish between an SSL server and a pure TCP relay). All other cases will
815 * call it with a proper error status like HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, HCHK_STATUS_L6RSP,
816 * etc.
817 *
818 * Please do NOT place any return statement in this function and only leave
819 * via the out label.
820 *
821 * This must be called with the server lock held.
822 */
823static void __event_srv_chk_r(struct conn_stream *cs)
824{
825 struct connection *conn = cs->conn;
826 struct check *check = cs->data;
827 struct server *s = check->server;
828 struct task *t = check->task;
829 char *desc;
830 int done;
831 unsigned short msglen;
832
833 if (unlikely(check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED)(__builtin_expect((check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED) != 0, 0
)))
834 goto out_wakeup;
835
836 /* wake() will take care of calling tcpcheck_main() */
837 if (check->type == PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000)
838 goto out;
839
840 /* Warning! Linux returns EAGAIN on SO_ERROR if data are still available
841 * but the connection was closed on the remote end. Fortunately, recv still
842 * works correctly and we don't need to do the getsockopt() on linux.
843 */
844
845 /* Set buffer to point to the end of the data already read, and check
846 * that there is free space remaining. If the buffer is full, proceed
847 * with running the checks without attempting another socket read.
848 */
849
850 done = 0;
851
852 cs->conn->mux->rcv_buf(cs, &check->bi, b_size(&check->bi), 0);
853 if (conn->flags & (CO_FL_ERROR | CO_FL_SOCK_RD_SH) || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR) {
854 done = 1;
855 if ((conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR) && !b_data(&check->bi)) {
856 /* Report network errors only if we got no other data. Otherwise
857 * we'll let the upper layers decide whether the response is OK
858 * or not. It is very common that an RST sent by the server is
859 * reported as an error just after the last data chunk.
860 */
861 chk_report_conn_err(check, errno(*__errno_location ()), 0);
862 goto out_wakeup;
863 }
864 }
865
866 /* the rest of the code below expects the connection to be ready! */
867 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_XPRT && !done)
868 goto wait_more_data;
869
870 /* Intermediate or complete response received.
871 * Terminate string in b_head(&check->bi) buffer.
872 */
873 if (b_data(&check->bi) < b_size(&check->bi))
874 b_head(&check->bi)[b_data(&check->bi)] = '\0';
875 else {
876 b_head(&check->bi)[b_data(&check->bi) - 1] = '\0';
877 done = 1; /* buffer full, don't wait for more data */
878 }
879
880 /* Run the checks... */
881 switch (check->type) {
882 case PR_O2_HTTP_CHK0x40000000:
883 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < strlen("HTTP/1.0 000\r"))
884 goto wait_more_data;
885
886 /* Check if the server speaks HTTP 1.X */
887 if ((b_data(&check->bi) < strlen("HTTP/1.0 000\r")) ||
888 (memcmp(b_head(&check->bi), "HTTP/1.", 7) != 0 ||
889 (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 12) != ' ' && *(b_head(&check->bi) + 12) != '\r')) ||
890 !isdigit((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 9))((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check
->bi) + 9)))] & (unsigned short int) _ISdigit) || !isdigit((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 10))((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check
->bi) + 10)))] & (unsigned short int) _ISdigit) ||
891 !isdigit((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 11))((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check
->bi) + 11)))] & (unsigned short int) _ISdigit)) {
892 cut_crlf(b_head(&check->bi));
893 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, b_head(&check->bi));
894
895 goto out_wakeup;
896 }
897
898 check->code = str2uic(b_head(&check->bi) + 9);
899 desc = ltrim(b_head(&check->bi) + 12, ' ');
900
901 if ((s->proxy->options & PR_O_DISABLE4040x40000000) &&
902 (s->next_state != SRV_ST_STOPPED) && (check->code == 404)) {
903 /* 404 may be accepted as "stopping" only if the server was up */
904 cut_crlf(desc);
905 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKCD, desc);
906 }
907 else if (s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_EXP_TYPE0x03800000) {
908 /* Run content verification check... We know we have at least 13 chars */
909 if (!httpchk_expect(s, done))
910 goto wait_more_data;
911 }
912 /* check the reply : HTTP/1.X 2xx and 3xx are OK */
913 else if (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 9) == '2' || *(b_head(&check->bi) + 9) == '3') {
914 cut_crlf(desc);
915 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, desc);
916 }
917 else {
918 cut_crlf(desc);
919 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, desc);
920 }
921 break;
922
923 case PR_O2_SSL3_CHK0x70000000:
924 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < 5)
925 goto wait_more_data;
926
927 /* Check for SSLv3 alert or handshake */
928 if ((b_data(&check->bi) >= 5) && (*b_head(&check->bi) == 0x15 || *b_head(&check->bi) == 0x16))
929 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6OK, NULL((void*)0));
930 else
931 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6RSP, NULL((void*)0));
932 break;
933
934 case PR_O2_SMTP_CHK0x30000000:
935 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < strlen("000\r"))
936 goto wait_more_data;
937
938 /* do not reset when closing, servers don't like this */
939 if (conn_ctrl_ready(cs->conn))
940 fdtab[cs->conn->handle.fd].linger_risk = 0;
941
942 /* Check if the server speaks SMTP */
943 if ((b_data(&check->bi) < strlen("000\r")) ||
944 (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 3) != ' ' && *(b_head(&check->bi) + 3) != '\r') ||
945 !isdigit((unsigned char) *b_head(&check->bi))((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *b_head(&check
->bi)))] & (unsigned short int) _ISdigit) || !isdigit((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 1))((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check
->bi) + 1)))] & (unsigned short int) _ISdigit) ||
946 !isdigit((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 2))((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char) *(b_head(&check
->bi) + 2)))] & (unsigned short int) _ISdigit)) {
947 cut_crlf(b_head(&check->bi));
948 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, b_head(&check->bi));
949 goto out_wakeup;
950 }
951
952 check->code = str2uic(b_head(&check->bi));
953
954 desc = ltrim(b_head(&check->bi) + 3, ' ');
955 cut_crlf(desc);
956
957 /* Check for SMTP code 2xx (should be 250) */
958 if (*b_head(&check->bi) == '2')
959 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, desc);
960 else
961 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, desc);
962 break;
963
964 case PR_O2_LB_AGENT_CHK0x80000000: {
965 int status = HCHK_STATUS_CHECKED;
966 const char *hs = NULL((void*)0); /* health status */
967 const char *as = NULL((void*)0); /* admin status */
968 const char *ps = NULL((void*)0); /* performance status */
969 const char *cs = NULL((void*)0); /* maxconn */
970 const char *err = NULL((void*)0); /* first error to report */
971 const char *wrn = NULL((void*)0); /* first warning to report */
972 char *cmd, *p;
973
974 /* We're getting an agent check response. The agent could
975 * have been disabled in the mean time with a long check
976 * still pending. It is important that we ignore the whole
977 * response.
978 */
979 if (!(check->server->agent.state & CHK_ST_ENABLED0x0004))
980 break;
981
982 /* The agent supports strings made of a single line ended by the
983 * first CR ('\r') or LF ('\n'). This line is composed of words
984 * delimited by spaces (' '), tabs ('\t'), or commas (','). The
985 * line may optionally contained a description of a state change
986 * after a sharp ('#'), which is only considered if a health state
987 * is announced.
988 *
989 * Words may be composed of :
990 * - a numeric weight suffixed by the percent character ('%').
991 * - a health status among "up", "down", "stopped", and "fail".
992 * - an admin status among "ready", "drain", "maint".
993 *
994 * These words may appear in any order. If multiple words of the
995 * same category appear, the last one wins.
996 */
997
998 p = b_head(&check->bi);
999 while (*p && *p != '\n' && *p != '\r')
1000 p++;
1001
1002 if (!*p) {
1003 if (!done)
1004 goto wait_more_data;
1005
1006 /* at least inform the admin that the agent is mis-behaving */
1007 set_server_check_status(check, check->status, "Ignoring incomplete line from agent");
1008 break;
1009 }
1010
1011 *p = 0;
1012 cmd = b_head(&check->bi);
1013
1014 while (*cmd) {
1015 /* look for next word */
1016 if (*cmd == ' ' || *cmd == '\t' || *cmd == ',') {
1017 cmd++;
1018 continue;
1019 }
1020
1021 if (*cmd == '#') {
1022 /* this is the beginning of a health status description,
1023 * skip the sharp and blanks.
1024 */
1025 cmd++;
1026 while (*cmd == '\t' || *cmd == ' ')
1027 cmd++;
1028 break;
1029 }
1030
1031 /* find the end of the word so that we have a null-terminated
1032 * word between <cmd> and <p>.
1033 */
1034 p = cmd + 1;
1035 while (*p && *p != '\t' && *p != ' ' && *p != '\n' && *p != ',')
1036 p++;
1037 if (*p)
1038 *p++ = 0;
1039
1040 /* first, health statuses */
1041 if (strcasecmp(cmd, "up") == 0) {
1042 check->health = check->rise + check->fall - 1;
1043 status = HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD;
1044 hs = cmd;
1045 }
1046 else if (strcasecmp(cmd, "down") == 0) {
1047 check->health = 0;
1048 status = HCHK_STATUS_L7STS;
1049 hs = cmd;
1050 }
1051 else if (strcasecmp(cmd, "stopped") == 0) {
1052 check->health = 0;
1053 status = HCHK_STATUS_L7STS;
1054 hs = cmd;
1055 }
1056 else if (strcasecmp(cmd, "fail") == 0) {
1057 check->health = 0;
1058 status = HCHK_STATUS_L7STS;
1059 hs = cmd;
1060 }
1061 /* admin statuses */
1062 else if (strcasecmp(cmd, "ready") == 0) {
1063 as = cmd;
1064 }
1065 else if (strcasecmp(cmd, "drain") == 0) {
1066 as = cmd;
1067 }
1068 else if (strcasecmp(cmd, "maint") == 0) {
1069 as = cmd;
1070 }
1071 /* try to parse a weight here and keep the last one */
1072 else if (isdigit((unsigned char)*cmd)((*__ctype_b_loc ())[(int) (((unsigned char)*cmd))] & (unsigned
short int) _ISdigit) && strchr(cmd, '%') != NULL((void*)0)) {
1073 ps = cmd;
1074 }
1075 /* try to parse a maxconn here */
1076 else if (strncasecmp(cmd, "maxconn:", strlen("maxconn:")) == 0) {
1077 cs = cmd;
1078 }
1079 else {
1080 /* keep a copy of the first error */
1081 if (!err)
1082 err = cmd;
1083 }
1084 /* skip to next word */
1085 cmd = p;
1086 }
1087 /* here, cmd points either to \0 or to the beginning of a
1088 * description. Skip possible leading spaces.
1089 */
1090 while (*cmd == ' ' || *cmd == '\n')
1091 cmd++;
1092
1093 /* First, update the admin status so that we avoid sending other
1094 * possibly useless warnings and can also update the health if
1095 * present after going back up.
1096 */
1097 if (as) {
1098 if (strcasecmp(as, "drain") == 0)
1099 srv_adm_set_drain(check->server);
1100 else if (strcasecmp(as, "maint") == 0)
1101 srv_adm_set_maint(check->server);
1102 else
1103 srv_adm_set_ready(check->server);
1104 }
1105
1106 /* now change weights */
1107 if (ps) {
1108 const char *msg;
1109
1110 msg = server_parse_weight_change_request(s, ps);
1111 if (!wrn || !*wrn)
1112 wrn = msg;
1113 }
1114
1115 if (cs) {
1116 const char *msg;
1117
1118 cs += strlen("maxconn:");
1119
1120 msg = server_parse_maxconn_change_request(s, cs);
1121 if (!wrn || !*wrn)
1122 wrn = msg;
1123 }
1124
1125 /* and finally health status */
1126 if (hs) {
1127 /* We'll report some of the warnings and errors we have
1128 * here. Down reports are critical, we leave them untouched.
1129 * Lack of report, or report of 'UP' leaves the room for
1130 * ERR first, then WARN.
1131 */
1132 const char *msg = cmd;
1133 struct buffer *t;
1134
1135 if (!*msg || status == HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD) {
1136 if (err && *err)
1137 msg = err;
1138 else if (wrn && *wrn)
1139 msg = wrn;
1140 }
1141
1142 t = get_trash_chunk();
1143 chunk_printf(t, "via agent : %s%s%s%s",
1144 hs, *msg ? " (" : "",
1145 msg, *msg ? ")" : "");
1146
1147 set_server_check_status(check, status, t->area);
1148 }
1149 else if (err && *err) {
1150 /* No status change but we'd like to report something odd.
1151 * Just report the current state and copy the message.
1152 */
1153 chunk_printf(&trash, "agent reports an error : %s", err);
1154 set_server_check_status(check, status/*check->status*/,
1155 trash.area);
1156
1157 }
1158 else if (wrn && *wrn) {
1159 /* No status change but we'd like to report something odd.
1160 * Just report the current state and copy the message.
1161 */
1162 chunk_printf(&trash, "agent warns : %s", wrn);
1163 set_server_check_status(check, status/*check->status*/,
1164 trash.area);
1165 }
1166 else
1167 set_server_check_status(check, status, NULL((void*)0));
1168 break;
1169 }
1170
1171 case PR_O2_PGSQL_CHK0x10000000:
1172 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < 9)
1173 goto wait_more_data;
1174
1175 /* do not reset when closing, servers don't like this */
1176 if (conn_ctrl_ready(cs->conn))
1177 fdtab[cs->conn->handle.fd].linger_risk = 0;
1178
1179 if (b_head(&check->bi)[0] == 'R') {
1180 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, "PostgreSQL server is ok");
1181 }
1182 else {
1183 if ((b_head(&check->bi)[0] == 'E') && (b_head(&check->bi)[5]!=0) && (b_head(&check->bi)[6]!=0))
1184 desc = &b_head(&check->bi)[6];
1185 else
1186 desc = "PostgreSQL unknown error";
1187
1188 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, desc);
1189 }
1190 break;
1191
1192 case PR_O2_REDIS_CHK0x20000000:
1193 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < 7)
1194 goto wait_more_data;
1195
1196 if (strcmp(b_head(&check->bi), "+PONG\r\n") == 0) {
1197 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, "Redis server is ok");
1198 }
1199 else {
1200 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, b_head(&check->bi));
1201 }
1202 break;
1203
1204 case PR_O2_MYSQL_CHK0x50000000:
1205 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < 5)
1206 goto wait_more_data;
1207
1208 /* do not reset when closing, servers don't like this */
1209 if (conn_ctrl_ready(cs->conn))
1210 fdtab[cs->conn->handle.fd].linger_risk = 0;
1211
1212 if (s->proxy->check_len == 0) { // old mode
1213 if (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 4) != '\xff') {
1214 /* We set the MySQL Version in description for information purpose
1215 * FIXME : it can be cool to use MySQL Version for other purpose,
1216 * like mark as down old MySQL server.
1217 */
1218 if (b_data(&check->bi) > 51) {
1219 desc = ltrim(b_head(&check->bi) + 5, ' ');
1220 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, desc);
1221 }
1222 else {
1223 if (!done)
1224 goto wait_more_data;
1225
1226 /* it seems we have a OK packet but without a valid length,
1227 * it must be a protocol error
1228 */
1229 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, b_head(&check->bi));
1230 }
1231 }
1232 else {
1233 /* An error message is attached in the Error packet */
1234 desc = ltrim(b_head(&check->bi) + 7, ' ');
1235 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, desc);
1236 }
1237 } else {
1238 unsigned int first_packet_len = ((unsigned int) *b_head(&check->bi)) +
1239 (((unsigned int) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 1)) << 8) +
1240 (((unsigned int) *(b_head(&check->bi) + 2)) << 16);
1241
1242 if (b_data(&check->bi) == first_packet_len + 4) {
1243 /* MySQL Error packet always begin with field_count = 0xff */
1244 if (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 4) != '\xff') {
1245 /* We have only one MySQL packet and it is a Handshake Initialization packet
1246 * but we need to have a second packet to know if it is alright
1247 */
1248 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < first_packet_len + 5)
1249 goto wait_more_data;
1250 }
1251 else {
1252 /* We have only one packet and it is an Error packet,
1253 * an error message is attached, so we can display it
1254 */
1255 desc = &b_head(&check->bi)[7];
1256 //ha_warning("onlyoneERR: %s\n", desc);
1257 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, desc);
1258 }
1259 } else if (b_data(&check->bi) > first_packet_len + 4) {
1260 unsigned int second_packet_len = ((unsigned int) *(b_head(&check->bi) + first_packet_len + 4)) +
1261 (((unsigned int) *(b_head(&check->bi) + first_packet_len + 5)) << 8) +
1262 (((unsigned int) *(b_head(&check->bi) + first_packet_len + 6)) << 16);
1263
1264 if (b_data(&check->bi) == first_packet_len + 4 + second_packet_len + 4 ) {
1265 /* We have 2 packets and that's good */
1266 /* Check if the second packet is a MySQL Error packet or not */
1267 if (*(b_head(&check->bi) + first_packet_len + 8) != '\xff') {
1268 /* No error packet */
1269 /* We set the MySQL Version in description for information purpose */
1270 desc = &b_head(&check->bi)[5];
1271 //ha_warning("2packetOK: %s\n", desc);
1272 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, desc);
1273 }
1274 else {
1275 /* An error message is attached in the Error packet
1276 * so we can display it ! :)
1277 */
1278 desc = &b_head(&check->bi)[first_packet_len+11];
1279 //ha_warning("2packetERR: %s\n", desc);
1280 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, desc);
1281 }
1282 }
1283 }
1284 else {
1285 if (!done)
1286 goto wait_more_data;
1287
1288 /* it seems we have a Handshake Initialization packet but without a valid length,
1289 * it must be a protocol error
1290 */
1291 desc = &b_head(&check->bi)[5];
1292 //ha_warning("protoerr: %s\n", desc);
1293 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, desc);
1294 }
1295 }
1296 break;
1297
1298 case PR_O2_LDAP_CHK0x60000000:
1299 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < 14)
1300 goto wait_more_data;
1301
1302 /* Check if the server speaks LDAP (ASN.1/BER)
1303 * http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basic_Encoding_Rules
1304 * http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4511
1305 */
1306
1307 /* http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4511#section-4.1.1
1308 * LDAPMessage: 0x30: SEQUENCE
1309 */
1310 if ((b_data(&check->bi) < 14) || (*(b_head(&check->bi)) != '\x30')) {
1311 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, "Not LDAPv3 protocol");
1312 }
1313 else {
1314 /* size of LDAPMessage */
1315 msglen = (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 1) & 0x80) ? (*(b_head(&check->bi) + 1) & 0x7f) : 0;
1316
1317 /* http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4511#section-4.2.2
1318 * messageID: 0x02 0x01 0x01: INTEGER 1
1319 * protocolOp: 0x61: bindResponse
1320 */
1321 if ((msglen > 2) ||
1322 (memcmp(b_head(&check->bi) + 2 + msglen, "\x02\x01\x01\x61", 4) != 0)) {
1323 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, "Not LDAPv3 protocol");
1324 goto out_wakeup;
1325 }
1326
1327 /* size of bindResponse */
1328 msglen += (*(b_head(&check->bi) + msglen + 6) & 0x80) ? (*(b_head(&check->bi) + msglen + 6) & 0x7f) : 0;
1329
1330 /* http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4511#section-4.1.9
1331 * ldapResult: 0x0a 0x01: ENUMERATION
1332 */
1333 if ((msglen > 4) ||
1334 (memcmp(b_head(&check->bi) + 7 + msglen, "\x0a\x01", 2) != 0)) {
1335 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7RSP, "Not LDAPv3 protocol");
1336 goto out_wakeup;
1337 }
1338
1339 /* http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4511#section-4.1.9
1340 * resultCode
1341 */
1342 check->code = *(b_head(&check->bi) + msglen + 9);
1343 if (check->code) {
1344 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, "See RFC: http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4511#section-4.1.9");
1345 } else {
1346 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, "Success");
1347 }
1348 }
1349 break;
1350
1351 case PR_O2_SPOP_CHK0xB0000000: {
1352 unsigned int framesz;
1353 char err[HCHK_DESC_LEN128];
1354
1355 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < 4)
1356 goto wait_more_data;
1357
1358 memcpy(&framesz, b_head(&check->bi), 4);
1359 framesz = ntohl(framesz)__bswap_32 (framesz);
1360
1361 if (!done && b_data(&check->bi) < (4+framesz))
1362 goto wait_more_data;
1363
1364 if (!spoe_handle_healthcheck_response(b_head(&check->bi)+4, framesz, err, HCHK_DESC_LEN128-1))
1365 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7OKD, "SPOA server is ok");
1366 else
1367 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L7STS, err);
1368 break;
1369 }
1370
1371 default:
1372 /* good connection is enough for pure TCP check */
1373 if (!(conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_XPRT) && !check->type) {
1374 if (check->use_ssl)
1375 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6OK, NULL((void*)0));
1376 else
1377 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L4OK, NULL((void*)0));
1378 }
1379 break;
1380 } /* switch */
1381
1382 out_wakeup:
1383 /* collect possible new errors */
1384 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR)
1385 chk_report_conn_err(check, 0, 0);
1386
1387 /* Reset the check buffer... */
1388 *b_head(&check->bi) = '\0';
1389 b_reset(&check->bi);
1390
1391 /* Close the connection... We still attempt to nicely close if,
1392 * for instance, SSL needs to send a "close notify." Later, we perform
1393 * a hard close and reset the connection if some data are pending,
1394 * otherwise we end up with many TIME_WAITs and eat all the source port
1395 * range quickly. To avoid sending RSTs all the time, we first try to
1396 * drain pending data.
1397 */
1398 /* Call cs_shutr() first, to add the CO_FL_SOCK_RD_SH flag on the
1399 * connection, to make sure cs_shutw() will not lead to a shutdown()
1400 * that would provoke TIME_WAITs.
1401 */
1402 cs_shutr(cs, CS_SHR_DRAIN);
1403 cs_shutw(cs, CS_SHW_NORMAL);
1404
1405 /* OK, let's not stay here forever */
1406 if (check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED)
1407 conn->flags |= CO_FL_ERROR;
1408
1409 task_wakeup(t, TASK_WOKEN_IO0x0400);
1410out:
1411 return;
1412
1413 wait_more_data:
1414 cs->conn->mux->subscribe(cs, SUB_RETRY_RECV, &check->wait_list);
1415 goto out;
1416}
1417
1418/*

1422 * connection (eg: reconnect).

1435
1436 /* we may have to make progress on the TCP checks */
1437 if (check->type == PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000) {

1441 } else {

1448 if (unlikely(conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR)(__builtin_expect((conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR || cs->
flags & CS_FL_ERROR) != 0, 0))) {
1449 /* We may get error reports bypassing the I/O handlers, typically
1450 * the case when sending a pure TCP check which fails, then the I/O
1451 * handlers above are not called. This is completely handled by the
1452 * main processing task so let's simply wake it up. If we get here,
1453 * we expect errno to still be valid.
1454 */
1455 chk_report_conn_err(check, errno(*__errno_location ()), 0);
1456 task_wakeup(check->task, TASK_WOKEN_IO0x0400);
1457 }
1458 else if (!(conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_XPRT) && !check->type) {
1459 /* we may get here if only a connection probe was required : we
1460 * don't have any data to send nor anything expected in response,
1461 * so the completion of the connection establishment is enough.
1462 */
1463 task_wakeup(check->task, TASK_WOKEN_IO0x0400);
1464 }
1465
1466 if (check->result != CHK_RES_UNKNOWN) {
1467 /* Check complete or aborted. If connection not yet closed do it
1468 * now and wake the check task up to be sure the result is
1469 * handled ASAP. */
1470 conn_sock_drain(conn);
1471 cs_close(cs);
1472 ret = -1;
1473 /* We may have been scheduled to run, and the
1474 * I/O handler expects to have a cs, so remove
1475 * the tasklet
1476 */
1477 tasklet_remove_from_tasklet_list(check->wait_list.tasklet);
1478 task_wakeup(check->task, TASK_WOKEN_IO0x0400);
1479 }
1480
1481 if (check->server)
1482 HA_SPIN_UNLOCK(SERVER_LOCK, &check->server->lock)( (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof(*(&check->server
->lock)) == 8) ? ({ ({ if (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof
(*(&check->server->lock)) == 8) { asm volatile("lock subq %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned
long)(0x0000000100000000ULL + 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"
); } else if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) == 4)
{ asm volatile("lock subl %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&check->
server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned int)(0x0000000100000000ULL
+ 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*(&
check->server->lock)) == 2) { asm volatile("lock subw %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned

); } else if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) == 1)
{ asm volatile("lock subb %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&check->

1487 * handler from touching its fd, and perform the FD polling updates ourselves
1488 */
1489 if (ret < 0)

1493}

1533/* returns the first NON-COMMENT tcp-check rule from list <list> or NULL if
1534 * none was found.
1535 */
1536static struct tcpcheck_rule *get_first_tcpcheck_rule(struct list *list)
1537{
1538 struct tcpcheck_rule *r;
1539
1540 list_for_each_entry(r, list, list)for (r = ((typeof(r))(((const char *)((list)->n)) - ((size_t
)&((typeof(r))((void*)0))->list))); &r->list !=
(list); r = ((typeof(r))(((const char *)(r->list.n)) - ((
size_t)&((typeof(r))((void*)0))->list)))) {
1541 if (r->action != TCPCHK_ACT_COMMENT)
1542 return r;
1543 }
1544 return NULL((void*)0);
1545}
1546
1547/*
1548 * establish a server health-check that makes use of a connection.
1549 *
1550 * It can return one of :
1551 * - SF_ERR_NONE if everything's OK and tcpcheck_main() was not called
1552 * - SF_ERR_UP if if everything's OK and tcpcheck_main() was called
1553 * - SF_ERR_SRVTO if there are no more servers
1554 * - SF_ERR_SRVCL if the connection was refused by the server
1555 * - SF_ERR_PRXCOND if the connection has been limited by the proxy (maxconn)
1556 * - SF_ERR_RESOURCE if a system resource is lacking (eg: fd limits, ports, ...)
1557 * - SF_ERR_INTERNAL for any other purely internal errors
1558 * - SF_ERR_CHK_PORT if no port could be found to run a health check on an AF_INET* socket
1559 * Additionally, in the case of SF_ERR_RESOURCE, an emergency log will be emitted.
1560 * Note that we try to prevent the network stack from sending the ACK during the
1561 * connect() when a pure TCP check is used (without PROXY protocol).
1562 */
1563static int connect_conn_chk(struct task *t)
1564{
1565 struct check *check = t->context;
1566 struct server *s = check->server;
1567 struct conn_stream *cs = check->cs;
1568 struct connection *conn = cs_conn(cs);
1569 struct protocol *proto;
1570 struct tcpcheck_rule *tcp_rule = NULL((void*)0);
1571 int ret;
1572 int connflags = 0;
1573
1574 /* we cannot have a connection here */
1575 if (conn)
1576 return SF_ERR_INTERNAL0x00008000;
1577
1578 /* tcpcheck send/expect initialisation */
1579 if (check->type == PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000) {
1580 check->current_step = NULL((void*)0);
1581 tcp_rule = get_first_tcpcheck_rule(check->tcpcheck_rules);
1582 }
1583
1584 /* prepare the check buffer.
1585 * This should not be used if check is the secondary agent check
1586 * of a server as s->proxy->check_req will relate to the
1587 * configuration of the primary check. Similarly, tcp-check uses
1588 * its own strings.
1589 */
1590 if (check->type && check->type != PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000 && !(check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010)) {
1591 b_putblk(&check->bo, s->proxy->check_req, s->proxy->check_len);
1592
1593 /* we want to check if this host replies to HTTP or SSLv3 requests
1594 * so we'll send the request, and won't wake the checker up now.
1595 */
1596 if ((check->type) == PR_O2_SSL3_CHK0x70000000) {
1597 /* SSL requires that we put Unix time in the request */
1598 int gmt_time = htonl(date.tv_sec)__bswap_32 (date.tv_sec);
1599 memcpy(b_head(&check->bo) + 11, &gmt_time, 4);
1600 }
1601 else if ((check->type) == PR_O2_HTTP_CHK0x40000000) {
1602 if (s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_CHK_SNDST0x00080000)
1603 b_putblk(&check->bo, trash.area,
1604 httpchk_build_status_header(s, trash.area, trash.size));
1605 /* prevent HTTP keep-alive when "http-check expect" is used */
1606 if (s->proxy->options2 & PR_O2_EXP_TYPE0x03800000)
1607 b_putist(&check->bo, ist("Connection: close\r\n")({ char *__x = (void *)("Connection: close\r\n"); (struct ist
){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("Connection: close\r\n"
) ? ((void *)"Connection: close\r\n" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }));
1608 b_putist(&check->bo, ist("\r\n")({ char *__x = (void *)("\r\n"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len
= __builtin_constant_p("\r\n") ? ((void *)"\r\n" == (void *)
0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for
(__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
1609 *b_tail(&check->bo) = '\0'; /* to make gdb output easier to read */
1610 }
1611 }
1612
1613 if ((check->type & PR_O2_LB_AGENT_CHK0x80000000) && check->send_string_len) {
1614 b_putblk(&check->bo, check->send_string, check->send_string_len);
1615 }
1616
1617 /* for tcp-checks, the initial connection setup is handled separately as
1618 * it may be sent to a specific port and not to the server's.
1619 */
1620 if (tcp_rule && tcp_rule->action == TCPCHK_ACT_CONNECT) {
1621 tcpcheck_main(check);
1622 return SF_ERR_UP0x0000b000;
1623 }
1624
1625 /* prepare a new connection */
1626 cs = check->cs = cs_new(NULL((void*)0));
1627 if (!check->cs)
1628 return SF_ERR_RESOURCE0x00007000;
1629 conn = cs->conn;
1630 /* Maybe there were an older connection we were waiting on */
1631 check->wait_list.events = 0;
1632 tasklet_set_tid(check->wait_list.tasklet, tid);
1633
1634
1635 if (!sockaddr_alloc(&conn->dst))
1636 return SF_ERR_RESOURCE0x00007000;
1637
1638 if (is_addr(&check->addr)) {
1639 /* we'll connect to the check addr specified on the server */
1640 *conn->dst = check->addr;
1641 }
1642 else {
1643 /* we'll connect to the addr on the server */
1644 *conn->dst = s->addr;
1645 }
1646
1647 if (s->check.via_socks4 && (s->flags & SRV_F_SOCKS4_PROXY0x0400)) {
1648 conn->send_proxy_ofs = 1;
1649 conn->flags |= CO_FL_SOCKS4;
1650 }
1651
1652 proto = protocol_by_family(conn->dst->ss_family);
1653 conn->target = &s->obj_type;
1654
1655 if ((conn->dst->ss_family == AF_INET2) || (conn->dst->ss_family == AF_INET610)) {
1656 int i = 0;
1657
1658 i = srv_check_healthcheck_port(check);
1659 if (i == 0)
1660 return SF_ERR_CHK_PORT0x0000c000;
1661
1662 set_host_port(conn->dst, i);
1663 }
1664
1665 /* no client address */
1666
1667 conn_prepare(conn, proto, check->xprt);
1668 if (conn_install_mux(conn, &mux_pt_ops, cs, s->proxy, NULL((void*)0)) < 0)
1669 return SF_ERR_RESOURCE0x00007000;
1670 cs_attach(cs, check, &check_conn_cb);
1671
1672 /* only plain tcp-check supports quick ACK */
1673 if (check->type != 0)
1674 connflags |= CONNECT_HAS_DATA0x00000001;
1675 if ((check->type == 0 || check->type == PR_O2_TCPCHK_CHK0x90000000) &&
1676 (!tcp_rule || tcp_rule->action != TCPCHK_ACT_EXPECT))
1677 connflags |= CONNECT_DELACK_ALWAYS0x00000004;
1678
1679 ret = SF_ERR_INTERNAL0x00008000;
1680 if (proto && proto->connect)
1681 ret = proto->connect(conn, connflags);
1682
1683
1684#ifdef USE_OPENSSL1
1685 if (ret == SF_ERR_NONE0x00000000) {
1686 if (s->check.sni)
1687 ssl_sock_set_servername(conn, s->check.sni);
1688 if (s->check.alpn_str)
1689 ssl_sock_set_alpn(conn, (unsigned char *)s->check.alpn_str,
1690 s->check.alpn_len);
1691 }
1692#endif
1693 if (s->check.send_proxy && !(check->state & CHK_ST_AGENT0x0010)) {
1694 conn->send_proxy_ofs = 1;
1695 conn->flags |= CO_FL_SEND_PROXY;
1696 }
1697 if (conn->flags & (CO_FL_SEND_PROXY | CO_FL_SOCKS4) &&
1698 conn_ctrl_ready(conn)) {
1699 if (xprt_add_hs(conn) < 0)
1700 ret = SF_ERR_RESOURCE0x00007000;
1701 }
1702
1703 return ret;
1704}

)) == 4) ? ({ ({ if (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof(*(&
pid_list_lock)) == 8) { asm volatile("lock subq %1, %0\n" : "+m"
(*(&pid_list_lock)) : "er" ((unsigned long)(0x00010000 +
0x00000004)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*(&pid_list_lock
)) == 4) { asm volatile("lock subl %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&pid_list_lock
)) : "er" ((unsigned int)(0x00010000 + 0x00000004)) : "cc"); }
else if (sizeof(*(&pid_list_lock)) == 2) { asm volatile(
"lock subw %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&pid_list_lock)) : "er" ((
unsigned short)(0x00010000 + 0x00000004)) : "cc"); } else if (
sizeof(*(&pid_list_lock)) == 1) { asm volatile("lock subb %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&pid_list_lock)) : "er" ((unsigned char)(0x00010000
+ 0x00000004)) : "cc"); } else { void __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_sub__

("src/checks.c",1756); } }); }) : ({ void __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_drop_s__
(char *,int); if (sizeof(*(&pid_list_lock)) != 4 &&
(sizeof(long) != 8 || sizeof(*(&pid_list_lock)) != 8)) __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_drop_s__
("src/checks.c",1756); }) );
1757
1758 if (!elem->exited)
1759 kill(elem->pid, SIGTERM15);
1760
1761 check = elem->t->context;
1762 check->curpid = NULL((void*)0);
1763 pool_free(pool_head_pid_list, elem);
1764}

1783
1784static void sigchld_handler(struct sig_handler *sh)
1785{
1786 pid_t pid;
1787 int status;
1788
1789 while ((pid = waitpid(0, &status, WNOHANG1)) > 0)
1790 pid_list_expire(pid, status);
1791}
1792
1793static int init_pid_list(void)
1794{
1795 if (pool_head_pid_list != NULL((void*)0))
1796 /* Nothing to do */
1797 return 0;
1798
1799 if (!signal_register_fct(SIGCHLD17, sigchld_handler, SIGCHLD17)) {
1800 ha_alert("Failed to set signal handler for external health checks: %s. Aborting.\n",
1801 strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
1802 return 1;
1803 }
1804
1805 pool_head_pid_list = create_pool("pid_list", sizeof(struct pid_list), MEM_F_SHARED0x1);
1806 if (pool_head_pid_list == NULL((void*)0)) {
1807 ha_alert("Failed to allocate memory pool for external health checks: %s. Aborting.\n",
1808 strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
1809 return 1;
1810 }
1811
1812 return 0;
1813}
1814
1815/* helper macro to set an environment variable and jump to a specific label on failure. */
1816#define EXTCHK_SETENV(check, envidx, value, fail){ if (extchk_setenv(check, envidx, value)) goto fail; } { if (extchk_setenv(check, envidx, value)) goto fail; }
1817
1818/*
1819 * helper function to allocate enough memory to store an environment variable.
1820 * It will also check that the environment variable is updatable, and silently
1821 * fail if not.
1822 */
1823static int extchk_setenv(struct check *check, int idx, const char *value)
1824{
1825 int len, ret;
1826 char *envname;
1827 int vmaxlen;
1828
1829 if (idx < 0 || idx >= EXTCHK_SIZE) {
1830 ha_alert("Illegal environment variable index %d. Aborting.\n", idx);
1831 return 1;
1832 }
1833
1834 envname = extcheck_envs[idx].name;
1835 vmaxlen = extcheck_envs[idx].vmaxlen;
1836
1837 /* Check if the environment variable is already set, and silently reject
1838 * the update if this one is not updatable. */
1839 if ((vmaxlen == EXTCHK_SIZE_EVAL_INIT0) && (check->envp[idx]))
1840 return 0;
1841
1842 /* Instead of sending NOT_USED, sending an empty value is preferable */
1843 if (strcmp(value, "NOT_USED") == 0) {
1844 value = "";
1845 }
1846
1847 len = strlen(envname) + 1;
1848 if (vmaxlen == EXTCHK_SIZE_EVAL_INIT0)
1849 len += strlen(value);
1850 else
1851 len += vmaxlen;
1852
1853 if (!check->envp[idx])
1854 check->envp[idx] = malloc(len + 1);
1855
1856 if (!check->envp[idx]) {
1857 ha_alert("Failed to allocate memory for the environment variable '%s'. Aborting.\n", envname);
1858 return 1;
1859 }
1860 ret = snprintf(check->envp[idx], len + 1, "%s=%s", envname, value);
1861 if (ret < 0) {
1862 ha_alert("Failed to store the environment variable '%s'. Reason : %s. Aborting.\n", envname, strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
1863 return 1;
1864 }
1865 else if (ret > len) {
1866 ha_alert("Environment variable '%s' was truncated. Aborting.\n", envname);
1867 return 1;
1868 }
1869 return 0;
1870}
1871
1872static int prepare_external_check(struct check *check)
1873{
1874 struct server *s = check->server;
1875 struct proxy *px = s->proxy;
1876 struct listener *listener = NULL((void*)0), *l;
1877 int i;
1878 const char *path = px->check_path ? px->check_path : DEF_CHECK_PATH"";
1879 char buf[256];
1880
1881 list_for_each_entry(l, &px->conf.listeners, by_fe)for (l = ((typeof(l))(((const char *)((&px->conf.listeners
)->n)) - ((size_t)&((typeof(l))((void*)0))->by_fe))
); &l->by_fe != (&px->conf.listeners); l = ((typeof
(l))(((const char *)(l->by_fe.n)) - ((size_t)&((typeof
(l))((void*)0))->by_fe))))
1882 /* Use the first INET, INET6 or UNIX listener */
1883 if (l->addr.ss_family == AF_INET2 ||
1884 l->addr.ss_family == AF_INET610 ||
1885 l->addr.ss_family == AF_UNIX1) {
1886 listener = l;
1887 break;
1888 }
1889
1890 check->curpid = NULL((void*)0);
1891 check->envp = calloc((EXTCHK_SIZE + 1), sizeof(char *));
1892 if (!check->envp) {
1893 ha_alert("Failed to allocate memory for environment variables. Aborting\n");
1894 goto err;
1895 }
1896
1897 check->argv = calloc(6, sizeof(char *));
1898 if (!check->argv) {
1899 ha_alert("Starting [%s:%s] check: out of memory.\n", px->id, s->id);
1900 goto err;
1901 }
1902
1903 check->argv[0] = px->check_command;
1904
1905 if (!listener) {
1906 check->argv[1] = strdup("NOT_USED");
1907 check->argv[2] = strdup("NOT_USED");
1908 }
1909 else if (listener->addr.ss_family == AF_INET2 ||
1910 listener->addr.ss_family == AF_INET610) {
1911 addr_to_str(&listener->addr, buf, sizeof(buf));
1912 check->argv[1] = strdup(buf);
1913 port_to_str(&listener->addr, buf, sizeof(buf));
1914 check->argv[2] = strdup(buf);
1915 }
1916 else if (listener->addr.ss_family == AF_UNIX1) {
1917 const struct sockaddr_un *un;
1918
1919 un = (struct sockaddr_un *)&listener->addr;
1920 check->argv[1] = strdup(un->sun_path);
1921 check->argv[2] = strdup("NOT_USED");
1922 }
1923 else {
1924 ha_alert("Starting [%s:%s] check: unsupported address family.\n", px->id, s->id);
1925 goto err;
1926 }
1927
1928 addr_to_str(&s->addr, buf, sizeof(buf));
1929 check->argv[3] = strdup(buf);
1930
1931 if (s->addr.ss_family == AF_INET2 || s->addr.ss_family == AF_INET610)
1932 snprintf(buf, sizeof(buf), "%u", s->svc_port);
1933 else
1934 *buf = 0;
1935 check->argv[4] = strdup(buf);
1936
1937 for (i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
1938 if (!check->argv[i]) {
1939 ha_alert("Starting [%s:%s] check: out of memory.\n", px->id, s->id);
1940 goto err;
1941 }
1942 }
1943
1944 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_PATH, path, err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_PATH, path)) goto err; };
1945 /* Add proxy environment variables */
1946 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_NAME, px->id, err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_NAME, px->
id)) goto err; };
1947 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_ID, ultoa_r(px->uuid, buf, sizeof(buf)), err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_ID, ultoa_r(px
->uuid, buf, sizeof(buf)))) goto err; };
1948 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_ADDR, check->argv[1], err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_ADDR, check->
argv[1])) goto err; };
1949 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_PORT, check->argv[2], err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_PROXY_PORT, check->
argv[2])) goto err; };
1950 /* Add server environment variables */
1951 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_NAME, s->id, err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_NAME, s->
id)) goto err; };
1952 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_ID, ultoa_r(s->puid, buf, sizeof(buf)), err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_ID, ultoa_r(
s->puid, buf, sizeof(buf)))) goto err; };
1953 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_ADDR, check->argv[3], err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_ADDR, check->
argv[3])) goto err; };
1954 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_PORT, check->argv[4], err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_PORT, check->
argv[4])) goto err; };
1955 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_MAXCONN, ultoa_r(s->maxconn, buf, sizeof(buf)), err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_MAXCONN, ultoa_r
(s->maxconn, buf, sizeof(buf)))) goto err; };
1956 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_CURCONN, ultoa_r(s->cur_sess, buf, sizeof(buf)), err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_CURCONN, ultoa_r
(s->cur_sess, buf, sizeof(buf)))) goto err; };
1957
1958 /* Ensure that we don't leave any hole in check->envp */
1959 for (i = 0; i < EXTCHK_SIZE; i++)
1960 if (!check->envp[i])
1961 EXTCHK_SETENV(check, i, "", err){ if (extchk_setenv(check, i, "")) goto err; };
1962
1963 return 1;
1964err:
1965 if (check->envp) {
1966 for (i = 0; i < EXTCHK_SIZE; i++)
1967 free(check->envp[i]);
1968 free(check->envp);
1969 check->envp = NULL((void*)0);
1970 }
1971
1972 if (check->argv) {
1973 for (i = 1; i < 5; i++)
1974 free(check->argv[i]);
1975 free(check->argv);
1976 check->argv = NULL((void*)0);
1977 }
1978 return 0;
1979}
1980
1981/*
1982 * establish a server health-check that makes use of a process.
1983 *
1984 * It can return one of :
1985 * - SF_ERR_NONE if everything's OK
1986 * - SF_ERR_RESOURCE if a system resource is lacking (eg: fd limits, ports, ...)
1987 * Additionally, in the case of SF_ERR_RESOURCE, an emergency log will be emitted.
1988 *
1989 * Blocks and then unblocks SIGCHLD
1990 */
1991static int connect_proc_chk(struct task *t)
1992{
1993 char buf[256];
1994 struct check *check = t->context;
1995 struct server *s = check->server;
1996 struct proxy *px = s->proxy;
1997 int status;
1998 pid_t pid;
1999
2000 status = SF_ERR_RESOURCE0x00007000;
2001
2002 block_sigchld();
2003
2004 pid = fork();
2005 if (pid < 0) {
2006 ha_alert("Failed to fork process for external health check%s: %s. Aborting.\n",
2007 (global.tune.options & GTUNE_INSECURE_FORK(1<<16)) ?
2008 "" : " (likely caused by missing 'insecure-fork-wanted')",
2009 strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
2010 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_SOCKERR, strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
2011 goto out;
2012 }
2013 if (pid == 0) {
2014 /* Child */
2015 extern char **environ;
2016 struct rlimit limit;
2017 int fd;
2018
2019 /* close all FDs. Keep stdin/stdout/stderr in verbose mode */
2020 fd = (global.mode & (MODE_QUIET0x04|MODE_VERBOSE0x10)) == MODE_QUIET0x04 ? 0 : 3;
2021
2022 my_closefrom(fd);
2023
2024 /* restore the initial FD limits */
2025 limit.rlim_cur = rlim_fd_cur_at_boot;
2026 limit.rlim_max = rlim_fd_max_at_boot;
2027 if (setrlimit(RLIMIT_NOFILERLIMIT_NOFILE, &limit) == -1) {
2028 getrlimit(RLIMIT_NOFILERLIMIT_NOFILE, &limit);
2029 ha_warning("External check: failed to restore initial FD limits (cur=%u max=%u), using cur=%u max=%u\n",
2030 rlim_fd_cur_at_boot, rlim_fd_max_at_boot,
2031 (unsigned int)limit.rlim_cur, (unsigned int)limit.rlim_max);
2032 }
2033
2034 environ = check->envp;
2035 extchk_setenv(check, EXTCHK_HAPROXY_SERVER_CURCONN, ultoa_r(s->cur_sess, buf, sizeof(buf)));
2036 haproxy_unblock_signals();
2037 execvp(px->check_command, check->argv);
2038 ha_alert("Failed to exec process for external health check: %s. Aborting.\n",
2039 strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
2040 exit(-1);
2041 }
2042
2043 /* Parent */
2044 if (check->result == CHK_RES_UNKNOWN) {
2045 if (pid_list_add(pid, t) != NULL((void*)0)) {
2046 t->expire = tick_add(now_ms, MS_TO_TICKS(check->inter)(check->inter));
2047
2048 if (px->timeout.check && px->timeout.connect) {
2049 int t_con = tick_add(now_ms, px->timeout.connect);
2050 t->expire = tick_first(t->expire, t_con);
2051 }
2052 status = SF_ERR_NONE0x00000000;
2053 goto out;
2054 }
2055 else {
2056 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_SOCKERR, strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
2057 }
2058 kill(pid, SIGTERM15); /* process creation error */
2059 }
2060 else
2061 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_SOCKERR, strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
2062
2063out:
2064 unblock_sigchld();
2065 return status;
2066}

2090 * stopped, the server should not be checked or the check
2091 * is disabled.

2094 s->proxy->state == PR_STSTOPPED)

2102 ret = connect_proc_chk(t);
2103 if (ret == SF_ERR_NONE0x00000000) {
2104 /* the process was forked, we allow up to min(inter,
2105 * timeout.connect) for it to report its status, but
2106 * only when timeout.check is set as it may be to short
2107 * for a full check otherwise.
2108 */
2109 t->expire = tick_add(now_ms, MS_TO_TICKS(check->inter)(check->inter));
2110
2111 if (s->proxy->timeout.check && s->proxy->timeout.connect) {
2112 int t_con = tick_add(now_ms, s->proxy->timeout.connect);
2113 t->expire = tick_first(t->expire, t_con);
2114 }
2115 task_set_affinity(t, tid_bit);
2116 goto reschedule;
2117 }
2118
2119 /* here, we failed to start the check */
2120
2121 check->state &= ~CHK_ST_INPROGRESS0x0001;
2122 check_notify_failure(check);
2123
2124 /* we allow up to min(inter, timeout.connect) for a connection
2125 * to establish but only when timeout.check is set
2126 * as it may be to short for a full check otherwise
2127 */
2128 while (tick_is_expired(t->expire, now_ms)) {
2129 int t_con;
2130
2131 t_con = tick_add(t->expire, s->proxy->timeout.connect);
2132 t->expire = tick_add(t->expire, MS_TO_TICKS(check->inter)(check->inter));
2133
2134 if (s->proxy->timeout.check)
2135 t->expire = tick_first(t->expire, t_con);
2136 }
2137 }
2138 else {
2139 /* there was a test running.
2140 * First, let's check whether there was an uncaught error,
2141 * which can happen on connect timeout or error.
2142 */
2143 if (check->result == CHK_RES_UNKNOWN) {
2144 /* good connection is enough for pure TCP check */
2145 struct pid_list *elem = check->curpid;
2146 int status = HCHK_STATUS_UNKNOWN;
2147
2148 if (elem->exited) {
2149 status = elem->status; /* Save in case the process exits between use below */
2150 if (!WIFEXITED(status)(((status) & 0x7f) == 0))
2151 check->code = -1;
2152 else
2153 check->code = WEXITSTATUS(status)(((status) & 0xff00) >> 8);
2154 if (!WIFEXITED(status)(((status) & 0x7f) == 0) || WEXITSTATUS(status)(((status) & 0xff00) >> 8))
2155 status = HCHK_STATUS_PROCERR;
2156 else
2157 status = HCHK_STATUS_PROCOK;
2158 } else if (expired) {
2159 status = HCHK_STATUS_PROCTOUT;
2160 ha_warning("kill %d\n", (int)elem->pid);
2161 kill(elem->pid, SIGTERM15);
2162 }
2163 set_server_check_status(check, status, NULL((void*)0));
2164 }
2165
2166 if (check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED) {
2167 /* a failure or timeout detected */
2168 check_notify_failure(check);
2169 }
2170 else if (check->result == CHK_RES_CONDPASS) {
2171 /* check is OK but asks for stopping mode */
2172 check_notify_stopping(check);
2173 }
2174 else if (check->result == CHK_RES_PASSED) {
2175 /* a success was detected */
2176 check_notify_success(check);
2177 }
2178 task_set_affinity(t, 1);
2179 check->state &= ~CHK_ST_INPROGRESS0x0001;
2180
2181 pid_list_del(check->curpid);
2182
2183 rv = 0;
2184 if (global.spread_checks > 0) {
2185 rv = srv_getinter(check) * global.spread_checks / 100;
2186 rv -= (int) (2 * rv * (ha_random32() / 4294967295.0));
2187 }
2188 t->expire = tick_add(now_ms, MS_TO_TICKS(srv_getinter(check) + rv)(srv_getinter(check) + rv));
2189 }
2190
2191 reschedule:
2192 while (tick_is_expired(t->expire, now_ms))
2193 t->expire = tick_add(t->expire, MS_TO_TICKS(check->inter)(check->inter));
2194

server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned int)(0x0000000100000000ULL
+ 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*(&
check->server->lock)) == 2) { asm volatile("lock subw %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned

); } else if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) == 1)

+ 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"); } else { void __unsupported_argument_size_for_pl_sub__

2225 * stopped, the server should not be checked or the check
2226 * is disabled.

2250 * to establish but only when timeout.check is set

2257 t->expire = tick_first(t->expire, t_con);

2262 * if not connected, unless we didn't subscribe for
2263 * sending since otherwise we won't be woken up.

2279 /* should share same code than cases below */

2296 cs->conn->xprt_ctx,
2297 check->wait_list.events,
2298 &check->wait_list);
2299 /* We may have been scheduled to run, and the
2300 * I/O handler expects to have a cs, so remove
2301 * the tasklet
2302 */
2303 tasklet_remove_from_tasklet_list(check->wait_list.tasklet);
2304 cs_destroy(cs);
2305 cs = check->cs = NULL((void*)0);
2306 conn = NULL((void*)0);
2307 }
2308
2309 check->state &= ~CHK_ST_INPROGRESS0x0001;
2310 check_notify_failure(check);
2311
2312 /* we allow up to min(inter, timeout.connect) for a connection
2313 * to establish but only when timeout.check is set
2314 * as it may be to short for a full check otherwise
2315 */
2316 while (tick_is_expired(t->expire, now_ms)) {
2317 int t_con;
2318
2319 t_con = tick_add(t->expire, proxy->timeout.connect);
2320 t->expire = tick_add(t->expire, MS_TO_TICKS(check->inter)(check->inter));
2321
2322 if (proxy->timeout.check)
2323 t->expire = tick_first(t->expire, t_con);
2324 }
2325 }
2326 else {
2327 /* there was a test running.
2328 * First, let's check whether there was an uncaught error,
2329 * which can happen on connect timeout or error.
2330 */
2331 if (check->result == CHK_RES_UNKNOWN) {
2332 /* good connection is enough for pure TCP check */
2333 if (!(conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_XPRT) && !check->type) {
2334 if (check->use_ssl)
2335 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L6OK, NULL((void*)0));
2336 else
2337 set_server_check_status(check, HCHK_STATUS_L4OK, NULL((void*)0));
2338 }
2339 else if ((conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR) || cs->flags & CS_FL_ERROR || expired) {
2340 chk_report_conn_err(check, 0, expired);
2341 }
2342 else
2343 goto out_unlock; /* timeout not reached, wait again */
2344 }
2345
2346 /* check complete or aborted */
2347 if (conn && conn->xprt) {
2348 /* The check was aborted and the connection was not yet closed.
2349 * This can happen upon timeout, or when an external event such
2350 * as a failed response coupled with "observe layer7" caused the
2351 * server state to be suddenly changed.
2352 */
2353 conn_sock_drain(conn);
2354 cs_close(cs);
2355 }
2356
2357 if (cs) {
2358 if (check->wait_list.events)
2359 cs->conn->xprt->unsubscribe(cs->conn,
2360 cs->conn->xprt_ctx,
2361 check->wait_list.events,
2362 &check->wait_list);
2363 /* We may have been scheduled to run, and the
2364 * I/O handler expects to have a cs, so remove
2365 * the tasklet
2366 */
2367 tasklet_remove_from_tasklet_list(check->wait_list.tasklet);
2368 cs_destroy(cs);
2369 cs = check->cs = NULL((void*)0);
2370 conn = NULL((void*)0);
2371 }
2372
2373 if (check->server) {
2374 if (check->result == CHK_RES_FAILED) {
2375 /* a failure or timeout detected */
2376 check_notify_failure(check);
2377 }
2378 else if (check->result == CHK_RES_CONDPASS) {
2379 /* check is OK but asks for stopping mode */
2380 check_notify_stopping(check);
2381 }
2382 else if (check->result == CHK_RES_PASSED) {
2383 /* a success was detected */
2384 check_notify_success(check);
2385 }
2386 }
2387 task_set_affinity(t, MAX_THREADS_MASK(~0UL >> (((unsigned int)sizeof(long) * 8) - ((unsigned
int)sizeof(long) * 8))));
2388 check->state &= ~CHK_ST_INPROGRESS0x0001;
2389
2390 if (check->server) {
2391 rv = 0;
2392 if (global.spread_checks > 0) {
2393 rv = srv_getinter(check) * global.spread_checks / 100;
2394 rv -= (int) (2 * rv * (ha_random32() / 4294967295.0));
2395 }
2396 t->expire = tick_add(now_ms, MS_TO_TICKS(srv_getinter(check) + rv)(srv_getinter(check) + rv));
2397 }
2398 }
2399
2400 reschedule:
2401 while (tick_is_expired(t->expire, now_ms))
2402 t->expire = tick_add(t->expire, MS_TO_TICKS(check->inter)(check->inter));
2403 out_unlock:
2404 if (check->server)
2405 HA_SPIN_UNLOCK(SERVER_LOCK, &check->server->lock)( (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof(*(&check->server
->lock)) == 8) ? ({ ({ if (sizeof(long) == 8 && sizeof

: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned

{ asm volatile("lock subl %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&check->
server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned int)(0x0000000100000000ULL
+ 0x0000000000000004ULL)) : "cc"); } else if (sizeof(*(&
check->server->lock)) == 2) { asm volatile("lock subw %1, %0\n"
: "+m" (*(&check->server->lock)) : "er" ((unsigned

); } else if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) == 1)
{ asm volatile("lock subb %1, %0\n" : "+m" (*(&check->

(char *,int); if (sizeof(*(&check->server->lock)) !=

(&check->server->lock)) == 4) { asm volatile("lock subl %1, %0\n"
